	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php') != '6486319e2b343cf0f718684938fb30f1578ead4a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php') !== '6486319e2b343cf0f718684938fb30f1578ead4a') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php') !== '6486319e2b343cf0f718684938fb30f1578ead4a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusSessionHandler.class.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') != 'edb7aa5fbb93744b26c5eb0cd7037640ab82b73b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'edb7aa5fbb93744b26c5eb0cd7037640ab82b73b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'f7ec130f16c5498ce8c41131e669487b1ed43c04') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'edb7aa5fbb93744b26c5eb0cd7037640ab82b73b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '32af9ab0522b2b9d46dbe1e15a4b12ecb8bed27c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '32af9ab0522b2b9d46dbe1e15a4b12ecb8bed27c') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'd75989f12b41a283c5fa0bfbbe5d023aa38a8add') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '32af9ab0522b2b9d46dbe1e15a4b12ecb8bed27c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.js');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != '25bd5ed5805134acfdc2d984c9036a9ba911060a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '25bd5ed5805134acfdc2d984c9036a9ba911060a') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '1bf7fc9785fbd6464d97749b245fc952b40070dc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '25bd5ed5805134acfdc2d984c9036a9ba911060a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php') != 'bebb2c0dba07edf9991027128117b08900d5de18') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php') !== 'bebb2c0dba07edf9991027128117b08900d5de18') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php') !== '28887d0f0b4327c50634c56b9d70d7a72e8279ec') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php') !== 'bebb2c0dba07edf9991027128117b08900d5de18') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/200_viathinksoft_freeoid/gui.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

}
if (!is_file('whois/webwhois.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: whois/webwhois.php');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('whois/webwhois.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') != 'd25e7122dddf4a4824c5d26468aa010e188d675a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): whois/webwhois.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('whois/webwhois.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of whois/webwhois.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== 'd25e7122dddf4a4824c5d26468aa010e188d675a') {
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== 'f76efeef9c52e7e237e195835aba4baeecf8edcb') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: whois/webwhois.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('whois/webwhois.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('whois/webwhois.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('whois/webwhois.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('whois/webwhois.php') !== 'd25e7122dddf4a4824c5d26468aa010e188d675a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): whois/webwhois.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 6\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 6') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
